Alternatively, the program\r\nalso comes bundled in with a CLI-based GUI wizard which will help guide you through the program’s functionality.\r\n\r\nPERMISSIONS:\r\n\r\n** This program requires access to your file system. This program will scan your Minecraft world saves for convenience. Please grant the requested permissions when asked by the program or certain functionality may not work properly. You may change these settings later via the Windows 10 Settings app under the “Privacy” section. Due to UWP restrictions, this program will clone input world files into a local working cache directory, which is cleared by the program automatically. When converting worlds, the output is not currently customizable, so the program will tell you where you can find the converted result. Open this path in your file browser.\r\n\r\nFUNCTIONALITY INCLUDES:\r\nBedrock 1.0+ to Java Edition 1.12\r\nJava Edition 1.12 or Java Edition 1.13 to Bedrock\r\nJava Edition 1.13 to Java Edition: 1.12\r\n\r\nFAQ:\r\nQ: Does this convert block entities such as chests?\r\nA: Sort of. Some block entities like chests and their items are currently converted, but others may not work. Some currently intentionally non-implemented block entities include skulls, ender chests, and banners. Support for these will be progressively implemented in later updates. If your chests are not converting, please leave a report.\r\n\r\nQ: Does this support new Update Aquatic blocks?\r\nA: Full support for Minecraft 1.13 Update Aquatic blocks is currently in the works and will be in the next 0.4 update, along with 1.13 schematic support.\r\n\r\nQ: Why is this paid?\r\nA: It costs to publish to the Windows Store.
